<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Welcome!</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center">I’m Nina, a solo travel expert.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">I discovered my love of solo travel when I moved to Italy at 16. Since then, I’ve lived on 3 continents, visited 29 countries, and became a digital nomad.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">I started Nina Out and About to share my travel wisdom, and because my friends got tired of hearing my travel stories. Now I share my travel tips, guides, and funny mishaps to inspire other young women to turn their travel dreams into reality today!</p>
